Ok(String::from_utf8(buffer).map_err(|e| {\n792\t            prometheus::Error::Msg(format!(\"failed to convert metrics to UTF-8: {}\", e))\n793\t        })?)\n794\t    }\n795\t\n796\t    pub fn self.admin_session_revoked_total.clone()\n802\t    }\n803\t}\n804\t\n805\t/// Generate a short request ID from UUIDv7.\n806\t///\n807\t/// UUIDv7 provides time-ordered unique IDs. We take the first 8 hex characters,\n808\t/// hash them, and encode as hex for a short, URL-safe identifier.\n809\tpub fn generate_request_id() -> String {\n810\t    let uuid = Uuid::now_v7();\n811\t    let uuid_str = uuid.simple().to_string();\n812\t    // Take first 8 chars (enough entropy for uniqueness)\n813\t    let prefix = &uuid_str[..8];\n814\t\n815\t    // Hash to get a consistent short representation\n816\t    let mut hasher = DefaultHasher::new();\n817\t    prefix.hash(&mut hasher);\n818\t    let hash = hasher.finish();\n819\t\n820\t    // Encode as hex (16 chars = 64 bits)\n821\t    format!(\"{:016x}\", hash)\n822\t}\n823\t\n824\t/// Extension trait to add request ID extraction utilities.\n825\tpub trait RequestIdExt {\n826\t    fn get_request_id(&self) -> Option<String>;\n827\t    fn set_request_id(&mut self, id: &str);\n828\t}\n829\t\n830\timpl RequestIdExt for HeaderMap {\n831\t    fn get_request_id(&self) -> Option<String> {\n832\t        self.get(\"x-request-id\")\n833\t            .and_then(|v| v.to_str().ok())\n834\t            .map(|s| s.to_string())\n835\t    }\n836\t\n837\t    fn set_request_id(&mut self, id: &str) {\n838\t        if let Ok(val) = HeaderValue::from_str(id) {\n839\t            self.insert(\"x-request-id\", val);\n840\t        }\n841\t    }\n842\t}\n843\t\n844\t/// Guard that decrements the in-flight gauge when dropped.\n845\t///\n846\t/// This ensures that even if the handler panics, the in-flight count\n847\t/// is accurately decremented.\n848\tstruct InFlightGuard {\n849\t    metrics: Metrics,\n850\t}\n851\t\n852\timpl InFlightGuard {\n853\t    fn new(metrics: Metrics) -> Self {\n854\t        metrics.requests_in_flight.inc();\n855\t        tracing::trace!(requests_in_flight = metrics.requests_in_flight.get(), \"request started\");\n856\t        Self { metrics }\n857\t    }\n858\t}\n859\t\n860\timpl Drop for InFlightGuard {\n861\t    fn drop(&mut self) {\n862\t        self.metrics.requests_in_flight.dec();\n863\t        tracing::trace!(requests_in_flight = self.metrics.requests_in_flight.get(), \"request completed\");\n864\t    }\n865\t}\n866\t\n867\t/// Extract the path template from the matched route.\n868\t///\n869\t/// Axum's MatchedPath extractor provides the route template (e.g., \"/indexes/{uid}/search\")\n870\t/// instead of the actual path (e.g., \"/indexes/products/search\"), avoiding high-cardinality labels.\n871\tfn extract_path_template(request: &Request) -> String {\n872\t    request\n873\t        .extensions()\n874\t        .get::<axum::extract::MatchedPath>()\n875\t        .map(|mp| mp.as_str())\n876\t        .unwrap_or_else(|| request.uri().path())\n877\t        .to_string()\n878\t}\n879\t\n880\t/// Main middleware that combines request ID injection, structured logging, and Prometheus metrics.\n881\tpub async fn telemetry_middleware(\n882\t    State(telemetry): State<TelemetryState>,\n883\t    mut req: Request,\n884\t    next: Next,\n885\t) -> Response {\n886\t    let start = Instant::now();\n887\t    let method = req.method().clone();\n888\t    let path_template = extract_path_template(&req);\n889\t    let metrics = telemetry.metrics.clone();\n890\t    let pod_id = telemetry.pod_id.clone();\n891\t\n892\t    // Generate or extract request ID\n893\t    let request_id = req\n894\t        .headers()\n895\t        .get_request_id()\n896\t        .unwrap_or_else(generate_request_id);\n897\t    req.headers_mut().set_request_id(&request_id);\n898\t\n899\t    // Create span for structured logging with pod_id included.\n900\t    // Note: raw path is intentionally omitted to avoid logging index names\n901\t    // (which may contain customer identifiers). Use path_template instead.\n902\t    let span = info_span!(\n903\t        \"request\",\n904\t        request_id = %request_id,\n905\t        pod_id = %pod_id,\n906\t        method = %method,\n907\t        path_template = %path_template,\n908\t    );\n909\t\n910\t    let _guard = span.enter();\n911\t\n912\t    // Track in-flight requests\n913\t    let in_flight = InFlightGuard::new(metrics.clone());\n914\t\n915\t    let response = next.run(req).await;\n916\t\n917\t    drop(in_flight);\n918\t\n919\t    let status = response.status();\n920\t    let status_u16 = status.as_u16();\n921\t    let duration = start.elapsed();\n922\t\n923\t    // Record Prometheus metrics\n924\t    metrics\n925\t        .request_duration\n926\t        .with_label_values(&[method.as_str(), &path_template, &status_u16.to_string()])\n927\t        .observe(duration.as_secs_f64());\n928\t    metrics\n929\t        .requests_total\n930\t        .with_label_values(&[method.as_str(), &path_template, &status_u16.to_string()])\n931\t        .inc();\n932\t\n933\t    // Structured log entry (plan §10 shape)\n934\t    // Base fields: timestamp (from tracing-subscriber), level, message, duration_ms\n935\t    // Additional fields (index, node_count, estimated_hits, degraded)\n936\t    // are added by request handlers via the tracing span.\n937\t    let message = format!(\"{} {}\", method, status);\n938\t    if status.is_server_error() {\n939\t        tracing::error!(\n940\t            target: \"miroir.request\",\n941\t            pod_id = %pod_id,\n942\t            request_id = %request_id,\n943\t            message = %message,\n944\t            duration_ms = duration.as_millis() as u64,\n945\t            status = status_u16,\n946\t            method = %method,\n947\t            path_template = %path_template,\n948\t        );\n949\t    } else if status.is_client_error() {\n950\t        tracing::warn!(\n951\t            target: \"miroir.request\",\n952\t            pod_id = %pod_id,\n953\t            request_id = %request_id,\n954\t            message = %message,\n955\t            duration_ms = duration.as_millis() as u64,\n956\t            status = status_u16,\n957\t            method = %method,\n958\t            path_template = %path_template,\n959\t        );\n960\t    } else {\n961\t        tracing::info!(\n962\t            target: \"miroir.request\",\n963\t            pod_id = %pod_id,\n964\t            request_id = %request_id,\n965\t            message = %message,\n966\t            duration_ms = duration.as_millis() as u64,\n967\t            status = status_u16,\n968\t            method = %method,\n969\t            path_template = %path_template,\n970\t        );\n971\t    }\n972\t\n973\t    // Ensure request ID is in response headers\n974\t    let mut response = response;\n975\t    if !response.headers().contains_key(\"x-request-id\") {\n976\t        if let Ok(val) = HeaderValue::from_str(&request_id) {\n977\t            response.headers_mut().insert(\"x-request-id\", val);\n978\t        }\n979\t    }\n980\t\n981\t    response\n982\t}\n983\t\n984\t/// Create the metrics router for the :9090 server.\n985\tpub fn metrics_router() -> Router<Metrics> {\n986\t    Router::new().route(\"/metrics\", get(metrics_handler))\n987\t}\n988\t\n989\t/// Handler that returns P7.5 Structured JSON logging + request IDs + trace correlation tests.\n//!\n//! Tests for plan §10 structured logging format:\n//! - JSON-per-line parseable by jq\n//! - request_id on every log line (same as X-Request-Id header)\n//! - No PII (API keys, document content, query strings) in logs\n//! - Log volume: < 1 entry per request at INFO level\n\nuse axum::{\n    extract::Request,\n    body::Body,\n    http::StatusCode,\n    Router,\n};\nuse tower::ServiceExt;\n\n/// Helper: parse a JSON log line and extract fields\nfn parse_log_line(line: &str) -> Option<serde_json::Value> {\n    serde_json::from_str(line).ok()\n}\n\n/// Helper: check if a string is a valid 8-char hex request ID\nfn is_valid_request_id(s: &str) -> bool {\n    s.len() == 8 && s.chars().all(|c| c.is_ascii_hexdigit())\n}\n\n/// Helper: check if a line contains PII patterns\nfn contains_pii(line: &str) -> bool {\n    let lower = line.to_lowercase();\n    // Check for API key patterns\n    if lower.contains(\"api_key\") || lower.contains(\"apikey\") || lower.contains(\"api-key\") {\n        // Allow if it's just \"api_key_hash\" or similar\n        if !lower.contains(\"hash\") && !lower.contains(\"uid\") {\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n    // Check for master keys\n    if lower.contains(\"master\") && (lower.contains(\"key\") || lower.contains(\"secret\")) {\n        return true;\n    }\n    // Check for JWT tokens\n    if lower.contains(\"eyj\") && lower.len() > 100 {\n        // JWT base64 pattern\n        return true;\n    }\n    // Check for document content patterns (long text blocks in logs)\n    if line.len() > 5000 {\n        // Very long log line might contain document content\n        return true;\n    }\n    // Check for raw query strings\n    if lower.contains(\"q=\") && lower.len() > 200 {\n        return true;\n    }\n    false\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Acceptance Criterion 1: jq parses every log line\n//
